     function load() {

 			icon.image = "http://www.vanagonauts.com/assets/vanicon.png";
 			icon.iconSize = new GSize(24, 11);
 			icon.iconAnchor = new GPoint(12, 9);
 			icon.infoWindowAnchor = new GPoint(12, 5);
 	
   var opts =  {maxWidth:140};
  
  
       function createMarker(point,name, html) {
         var marker = new GMarker(point, icon);
         GEvent.addListener(marker, "click", function() {
           marker.openInfoWindowHtml(html, opts); 
         });
         return marker;
       }

       <tr valign="top">
        <td class="tdpadding">
         <br/>
         <span class="header">
          Welcome...
         </span>
         <br/>
         <br/>
         <span class="header">
          to the archive site of the famed Vanagon Mailing List.
         </span>
         <br/>
         <span class="content">
          <span class="content">
           <br/>
           <br/>
           This site is based on the collective experience of many members of the vanagon mailing list, through their postings to the list. These are folks who have been there, done that and lived to tell about it.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           This website is a work in progress. Not every section will have content. I left the chapter headers in place so folks would know what areas still need material, and hopefully send it along!
           <font color="red">
            <b>
             Please
             <a href="mailto:vanagon@gmail.com">
              email
             </a>
             any posts from the Vanagon List Archives or elsewhere that you have found to be accurate and useful.
            </b>
           </font>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           We have permission (Thanks TomC) to include archived articles posted
           <b>
            after
           </b>
           Tue, 7 Apr 1998 provided the post does not explicitly reserve rights.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Let's spread the knowledge!.
           <br/>
           <!--<br />
 <img src="assets/web/rescue_app_QR.png" align="left" text-align="center"><br />
 New in the Android Market, the Vanagon Rescue Squad app for Android phones. Scan the QR at left or search the Market for Vanagon.<br />
 -->
           <br/>
           <!-- <br />
 The contents are generally arranged in the same order as Bentley&reg; and each section will begin with an intro listing special tools or materials needed as well as part numbers where applicable.<br />
 <br />
 Categories can be added as well as unlimited sub-categories. This can be done by anyone with a net connection. Volunteers?<br />
 <br />
 Comments can be added to each article if those comments clarify some point or add info. These comments can then be rated by subsequent readers. Best ratings go to the top of the list, worst ones drop right off.<br />
 <br />
 <br />
 <br />
 <FONT COLOR="RED"><b>PROJECT NOTES:</b></FONT><br />
 This site is scripted with PhP on a PostgreSQL database, served from a dual 750Mhz Penguin running Red Hat Linux 7.5 on a DS3 connection to the net.<br />
 <br />
 <br />
 <FONT COLOR="RED"><b>Revision History</b></FONT><br />
 <br />
 <font size="-1"><br />
 <br />
 8-12-04 Added mod_rewrite to allow plain text links for search engines.<br />
 <br />
 2-18-04 Optimized database for speed. Setup indexing on the data tables. Will do when all the queries are scripted.<br />
 <br />
 12-2-03 Sorted Rescue List results by distance from you.<br />
 <br />
 11-30-03 Added events calendar. <br />
 <br />
 11-27-03 Indexed the zip data. Rescue searches are pretty fast now considering the huge amount of lat lon city state and zip data in the table.<br />
 <br />
 11-24-03 Filled in some holes in the zipcode database. Some zips had 0 for lat and lon.. Free data. You get what you pay for ;-)<br />
 <br />
 <br />
 11-19-03 Added Canadian Postal Codes to Vanagon Rescue Squad database. Sign up Canada!<br />
 <br />
 <br />
 11-04-03<br />
 Added "Printer Friendly" button to  print only the text and pictures without the header graphic and navigation. <br />
 <br />
 11-03-03<br />
 Recieved permission (Thanks TomC) to include archived articles posted <b>after</b> Tue, 7 Apr 1998 provided the post does not contain the phrase "All Rights Reserved."<br />
 <br />
 10-12-03<br />
 Added form for "Vanagon Rescue Squad" volunteers. Kind of like type2.com's AIRS. Need Canadian postal codes with lat & lon.<br />
 <br />
 9-28-03<br />
 Added Bogus or Brilliant voting on each comment. Most Brilliant rises to top.<br />
 <br />
 9-22-03<br />
 FWIW comments field on each article for feedback/corrections. <br />
 <br />
 9-15-03<br />
 image uploads.. now working (Image Magic installed on server). It will resample any image to fit on the site while preserving the original.<br />
 <br />
 9-14-03<br />
 Added Lee Roesner's header Graphic. Thanks Lee, Looks Great<br />
 <br />
 9-13-03<br />
 Added sub-category navigation on the bottom. This gives you links to everything below where you are without going back to the menu tree.<br />
 <br />
 9-5-03<br />
 Added  symptoms field. Library can be searched by symptom now. This really works well assuming all the articles have symptom information. Try searching "runs hot"<br />
 <br />
 9-9-03<br />
 Added a links page. Add our favorite websites.<br />
 <br />
 9-8-03<br />
 Search Engine works. Needs major tuning.<br />
 <br />
 5-03 ~ 9-03 <br />
 Started project. Got to Busses by the Beach...Went N Michigan camping. Back to building website.  Went Canada camping. Continued programming. Oh yeah and work.  <br />
 <br />
 -->
